msg:As far as an old five-star hotel is concerned, this kind of equipment is already very good ~ the facilities are still very new, and it is really fun to bring children to play in the family room. These points are worthy of recognition!
Unfortunately, the biggest failure was the "extremely noisy" and "noisy" sound of the large water pump machine outside the hotel window! I've been suffering from it all night!
From the moment you enter the room until you leave the room, the high-decibel sound of large machines running makes your whole head feel buzzing and painful! Logically speaking, in a building as high as the 14th floor, such a "noisy" noise should not be so clear, but it is true that the quality of a night's sleep is seriously affected by it. As soon as the window is opened, I want to breathe, but I don't know what's going on. "Deafening"! It is conceivable that if you are a guest living on a "lower floor", you will probably feel like you are being "attacked by a bomber"!
Therefore, for the few five-star hotels in Nanqiao Old Town with good reputations for many years, the hotel should give "serious attention" to this issue. Guests pay to have a rest, not to suffer such "noise pollution"! Low-quality sleep gives guests a very bad experience! I hope the person in charge of the hotel can live up to the "five-star" brand at the front desk and solve the "environmental pollution" around it as soon as possible! Whether it is the use of large machines, coordinating with them to adopt "staggered peak opening", or using other feasibility study methods to prevent "noise pollution" from poisoning hotel guests, it is a need for a long-established "five-star hotel" Provide a solution and a reasonable explanation and statement to the customer!

msg:This was my second time staying at this hotel. The room was quite satisfactory, but the buffet breakfast the next day had very few dishes and the service was even worse.

We stayed in two rooms, 1208 and 1212. The next day, the four children and their children went down to have breakfast. No one swiped the card at the door when I entered. After I sat down, a waiter came over and asked if the card was swiped? We said we didn't see anyone at the door, so we were asked to swipe our cards again. After swiping the card, a woman from the next class came over and asked if the card had been swiped. Yes, management is so chaotic.

There were very few breakfast items and the taste was poor. There was almost nothing to eat. After two bowls of porridge, I only gave the baby some fruit snacks. Breakfast ended at 10 o'clock, but it was not yet 10 o'clock. Around 9:50, four waiters were sweeping the floor next to our table. Yes, you read that right, four. It felt like they were trying to drive us away, so we couldn't eat any more and got up to leave. The waitress in black came and asked, how was the meal... what else could we do? She said she was still eating and that she had a baby. Now, why are you sweeping the floor like this? The head waitress replied: I didnâ€™t sweep under your table. Thatâ€™s a really good answer. Goodbye.

Finally, whoever wants to experience the 5-star buffet breakfast service should hurry up and check in. We donâ€™t want to come back again.
